* Isaiah 1

** Isaiah 1:1

Visio Isaiæ, filii Amos, quam vidit super Judam et Jerusalem, in diebus Oziæ, Joathan, Achaz, et Ezechiæ, regum Juda.  <div eID="gen18060" type="x-p"/>

Audite, cæli, et auribus percipe, terra, <l eID="gen18062" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18063"/>quoniam Dominus locutus est. <l eID="gen18063" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18064"/>Filios enutrivi, et exaltavi ; <l eID="gen18064" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18065"/>ipsi autem spreverunt me. <l eID="gen18065" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 1:4

** Isaiah 1:5

Super quo percutiam vos ultra, addentes prævaricationem ? <l eID="gen18076" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18077"/>omne caput languidum, <l eID="gen18077" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18078"/>et omne cor mœrens. <l eID="gen18078" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 1:6

A planta pedis usque ad verticem, <l eID="gen18079" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18080"/>non est in eo sanitas ; <l eID="gen18080" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18081"/>vulnus, et livor, et plaga tumens, <l eID="gen18081" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18082"/>non est circumligata, nec curata medicamine, <l eID="gen18082" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18083"/>neque fota oleo. <l eID="gen18083" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 1:7

Terra vestra deserta ; <l eID="gen18084" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18085"/>civitates vestræ succensæ igni : <l eID="gen18085" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18086"/>regionem vestram coram vobis alieni devorant, <l eID="gen18086" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18087"/>et desolabitur sicut in vastitate hostili. <l eID="gen18087" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 1:8

Et derelinquetur filia Sion <l eID="gen18088" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18089"/>ut umbraculum in vinea, <l eID="gen18089" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18090"/>et sicut tugurium in cucumerario, <l eID="gen18090" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18091"/>et sicut civitas quæ vastatur. <l eID="gen18091" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 1:9

Nisi Dominus exercituum <l eID="gen18092" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18093"/>reliquisset nobis semen, <l eID="gen18093" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18094"/>quasi Sodoma fuissemus, <l eID="gen18094" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18095"/>et quasi Gomorrha similes essemus. <l eID="gen18095" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 1:10

** Isaiah 1:11

** Isaiah 1:13

** Isaiah 1:14

Calendas vestras, et solemnitates vestras odivit anima mea : <l eID="gen18114" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18115"/>facta sunt mihi molesta ; laboravi sustinens. <l eID="gen18115" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 1:15

Et cum extenderitis manus vestras, avertam oculos meos a vobis, <l eID="gen18116" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18117"/>et cum multiplicaveritis orationem, non exaudiam : <l eID="gen18117" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18118"/>manus enim vestræ sanguine plenæ sunt. <l eID="gen18118" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 1:16

** Isaiah 1:17

** Isaiah 1:18

Et venite, et arguite me, dicit Dominus. <l eID="gen18126" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18127"/>Si fuerint peccata vestra ut coccinum, <l eID="gen18127" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18128"/>quasi nix dealbabuntur ; <l eID="gen18128" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18129"/>et si fuerint rubra quasi vermiculus, <l eID="gen18129" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18130"/>velut lana alba erunt. <l eID="gen18130" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 1:19

Si volueritis, et audieritis me, <l eID="gen18131" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18132"/>bona terræ comeditis. <l eID="gen18132" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 1:20

** Isaiah 1:21

** Isaiah 1:22

** Isaiah 1:23

** Isaiah 1:24

** Isaiah 1:25

** Isaiah 1:26

** Isaiah 1:27

** Isaiah 1:28

** Isaiah 1:29

** Isaiah 1:30

** Isaiah 1:31

* Isaiah 2

** Isaiah 2:1

Verbum quod vidit Isaias, filius Amos, super Juda et Jerusalem.  <div eID="gen18171" type="x-p"/>

** Isaiah 2:2

Et erit in novissimis diebus : <l eID="gen18173" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18174"/>præparatus mons domus Domini <l eID="gen18174" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18175"/>in vertice montium, <l eID="gen18175" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18176"/>et elevabitur super colles ; <l eID="gen18176" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18177"/>et fluent ad eum omnes gentes, <l eID="gen18177" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 2:3

et ibunt populi multi, et dicent : <l eID="gen18178" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18179"/>Venite, et ascendamus ad montem Domini, <l eID="gen18179" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18180"/>et ad domum Dei Jacob ; <l eID="gen18180" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18181"/>et docebit nos vias suas, <l eID="gen18181" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18182"/>et ambulabimus in semitis ejus, <l eID="gen18182" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18183"/>quia de Sion exibit lex, <l eID="gen18183" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18184"/>et verbum Domini de Jerusalem. <l eID="gen18184" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 2:4

Et judicabit gentes, <l eID="gen18185" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18186"/>et arguet populos multos ; <l eID="gen18186" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18187"/>et conflabunt gladios suos in vomeres, <l eID="gen18187" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18188"/>et lanceas suas in falces. <l eID="gen18188" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18189"/>Non levabit gens contra gentem gladium, <l eID="gen18189" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18190"/>nec exercebuntur ultra ad prælium. <l eID="gen18190" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 2:5

Domus Jacob, venite, <l eID="gen18191" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18192"/>et ambulemus in lumine Domini. <l eID="gen18192" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 2:6

Projecisti enim populum tuum, <l eID="gen18193" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18194"/>domum Jacob, <l eID="gen18194" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18195"/>quia repleti sunt ut olim, <l eID="gen18195" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18196"/>et augeres habuerunt ut Philisthiim, <l eID="gen18196" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18197"/>et pueris alienis adhæserunt. <l eID="gen18197" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 2:7

** Isaiah 2:8

Et repleta est terra ejus equis, <l eID="gen18200" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18201"/>et innumerabiles quadrigæ ejus. <l eID="gen18201" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18202"/>Et repleta est terra ejus idolis ; <l eID="gen18202" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18203"/>opus manuum suarum adoraverunt, <l eID="gen18203" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18204"/>quod fecerunt digiti eorum. <l eID="gen18204" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 2:11

** Isaiah 2:18

* Isaiah 3

** Isaiah 3:1

Ecce enim Dominator, Dominus exercituum, <l eID="gen18248" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18249"/>auferet a Jerusalem et a Juda <l eID="gen18249" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18250"/>validum et fortem, <l eID="gen18250" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18251"/>omne robur panis, et omne robor aquæ ; <l eID="gen18251" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 3:2

fortem, et virum bellatorem, <l eID="gen18252" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18253"/>judicem, et prophetam, et ariolum, et senem ; <l eID="gen18253" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 3:3

principem super quinquaginta, et honorabilem vultu et consiliarium, <l eID="gen18254" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18255"/>et sapientem de architectis, et prudentem eloquii mystici. <l eID="gen18255" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 3:4

Et dabo pueros principes eorum, <l eID="gen18256" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18257"/>et effeminati dominabuntur eis ; <l eID="gen18257" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 3:5

et irruet populus, vir ad virum, <l eID="gen18258" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18259"/>et unusquisque ad proximum suum ; <l eID="gen18259" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18260"/>tumultuabitur puer contra senem, <l eID="gen18260" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18261"/>et ignobilis contra nobilem. <l eID="gen18261" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 3:6

Apprehendet enim vir fratrem suum, <l eID="gen18262" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18263"/>domesticum patris sui : <l eID="gen18263" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18264"/>Vestimentum tibi est, princeps esto noster, <l eID="gen18264" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18265"/>ruina autem hæc sub manu tua. <l eID="gen18265" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 3:7

Respondebit in die illa, dicens : <l eID="gen18266" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18267"/>Non sum medicus, <l eID="gen18267" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18268"/>et in domo mea non est panis neque vestimentum : <l eID="gen18268" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18269"/>nolite constituere me principem populi. <l eID="gen18269" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 3:8

Ruit enim Jerusalem, et Judas concidit, <l eID="gen18270" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18271"/>quia lingua eorum et adinventiones eorum contra Dominum, <l eID="gen18271" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18272"/>ut provocarent oculos majestatis ejus. <l eID="gen18272" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 3:9

Agnitio vultus eorum respondit eis ; <l eID="gen18273" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18274"/>et peccatum suum quasi Sodoma prædicaverunt, nec absconderunt. <l eID="gen18274" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18275"/>Væ animæ eorum, quoniam reddita sunt eis mala ! <l eID="gen18275" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 3:10

Dicite justo quoniam bene, <l eID="gen18276" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18277"/>quoniam fructum adinventionum suarum comedet. <l eID="gen18277" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 3:11

Væ impio in malum ! <l eID="gen18278" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18279"/>retributio enim manuum ejus fiet ei. <l eID="gen18279" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 3:12

Populum meum exactores sui spoliaverunt, <l eID="gen18280" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18281"/>et mulieres dominatæ sunt eis. <l eID="gen18281" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18282"/>Popule meus, qui te beatum dicunt, ipsi te decipiunt, <l eID="gen18282" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen18283"/>et viam gressuum tuorum dissipant. <l eID="gen18283" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 3:13

** Isaiah 6:1

* Isaiah 7

** Isaiah 7:1

Et factum est in diebus Achaz, filii Joathan, filii Oziæ, regis Juda, ascendit Rasin, rex Syriæ, et Phacee, filius Romeliæ, rex Israël, in Jerusalem, ad præliandum contra eam : et non potuerunt

** Isaiah 7:2

debellare eam. Et nuntiaverunt domui David, dicentes : Requievit Syria super Ephraim. Et commotum est cor ejus, et cor populi ejus, sicut moventur ligna silvarum a facie venti.

** Isaiah 7:3

* Isaiah 20

** Isaiah 20:1

In anno quo ingressus est Thathan in Azotum, cum misisset eum Sargon, rex Assyriorum, et pugnasset contra Azotum, et cepisset eam :

** Isaiah 20:2

in tempore illo locutus est Dominus in manu Isaiæ, filii Amos, dicens : Vade, et solve saccum de lumbis tuis, et calceamenta tua tolle de pedibus tuis. Et fecit sic, vadens nudus et discalceatus.

** Isaiah 20:3

Et dixit Dominus : <div eID="gen19340" type="x-p"/> <lg sID="gen19341"/> <l level="1" sID="gen19342"/>Sicut ambulavit servus meus Isaias nudus et discalceatus, <l eID="gen19342" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen19343"/>trium annorum signum et portentum erit <l eID="gen19343" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen19344"/>super Ægyptum et super Æthiopiam ; <l eID="gen19344" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 20:4

sic minabit rex Assyriorum captivitatem Ægypti, <l eID="gen19345" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen19346"/>et transmigrationem Æthiopiæ, <l eID="gen19346" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen19347"/>juvenum et senum, nudam et discalceatam, discoopertis natibus, ad ignominiam Ægypti. <l eID="gen19347" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 20:5

Et timebunt, et confundentur <l eID="gen19348" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen19349"/>ab Æthiopia spe sua, <l eID="gen19349" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen19350"/>et ab Ægypto gloria sua. <l eID="gen19350" level="1"/>

* Isaiah 22

** Isaiah 22:1

** Isaiah 22:5

dies enim interfectionis, <l eID="gen19442" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen19443"/>et conculcationis, et fletuum, <l eID="gen19443" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen19444"/>Domino Deo exercituum, <l eID="gen19444" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen19445"/>in valle Visionis, <l eID="gen19445" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen19446"/>scrutans murum, <l eID="gen19446" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen19447"/>et magnificus super montem. <l eID="gen19447" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 22:6

** Isaiah 22:11

** Isaiah 22:12

** Isaiah 22:20

** Isaiah 23:14

et erunt negotiationes ejus et mercedes ejus sanctificatæ Domino : <l eID="gen19573" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen19574"/>non condentur neque reponentur, <l eID="gen19574" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen19575"/>quia his qui habitaverint coram Domino erit negotiatio ejus, <l eID="gen19575" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen19576"/>ut manducent in saturitatem, et vestiantur usque ad vetustatem.  <chapter eID="Isa.23"/>

* Isaiah 24

** Isaiah 24:1

* Isaiah 36

** Isaiah 36:1

Et factum est in quartodecimo anno regis Ezechiæ, ascendit Sennacherib, rex Assyriorum, super omnes civitates Juda munitas, et cepit eas.

** Isaiah 36:2

Et misit rex Assyriorum Rabsacen de Lachis in Jerusalem, ad regem Ezechiam in manu gravi : et stetit in aquæductu piscinæ superioris in via Agri fullonis.

** Isaiah 36:3

Et egressus est ad eum Eliacim, filius Helciæ, qui erat super domum, et Sobna scriba, et Joahe filius Asaph, a commentariis.

** Isaiah 36:4

Et dixit ad eos Rabsaces : Dicite Ezechiæ : Hæc dicit rex magnus, rex Assyriorum : Quæ est ista fiducia qua confidis ?

** Isaiah 36:5

aut quo consilio vel fortitudine rebellare disponis ? super quem habes fiduciam, quia recessisti a me ?

** Isaiah 36:6

Ecce confidis super baculum arundineum confractum istum, super Ægyptum ; cui si innixus fuerit homo, intrabit in manum ejus, et perforabit eam : sic Pharao, rex Ægypti, omnibus qui confidunt in eo.

** Isaiah 36:7

Quod si responderis mihi : In Domino Deo nostro confidimus ; nonne ipse est cujus abstulit Ezechias excelsa et altaria, et dixit Judæ et Jerusalem : Coram altari isto adorabitis ?

** Isaiah 36:8

Et nunc trade te domino meo, regi Assyriorum, et dabo tibi duo millia equorum, nec poteris ex te præbere ascensores eorum :

** Isaiah 36:9

et quomodo sustinebis faciem judicis unius loci ex servis domini mei minoribus ? Quod si confidis in Ægypto, in quadrigis et in equitibus,

** Isaiah 36:10

et nunc numquid sine Domino ascendi ad terram istam, ut disperderem eam ? Dominus dixit ad me : Ascende super terram istam, et disperde eam.  <div eID="gen20414" type="x-p"/>

** Isaiah 36:11

Et dixit Eliacim, et Sobna, et Joahe, ad Rabsacen : Loquere ad servos tuos syra lingua ; intelligimus enim ; ne loquaris ad nos judaice in auribus populi qui est super murum.

** Isaiah 36:12

Et dixit ad eos Rabsaces : Numquid ad dominum tuum et ad te misit me dominus meus, ut loquerer omnia verba ista ? et non potius ad viros qui sedent in muro, ut comedant stercora sua, et bibant urinam pedum suorum vobiscum ?

** Isaiah 36:13

Et stetit Rabsaces, et clamavit voce magna judaice, et dixit : Audite verba regis magni, regis Assyriorum !

** Isaiah 36:14

Hæc dicit rex : Non seducat vos Ezechias, quia non poterit eruere vos.

** Isaiah 36:15

Et non vobis tribuat fiduciam Ezechias super Domino, dicens : Eruens liberabit nos Dominus : non dabitur civitas ista in manu regis Assyriorum.

** Isaiah 36:16

Nolite audire Ezechiam ; hæc enim dicit rex Assyriorum : Facite mecum benedictionem, et egredimini ad me, et comedite unusquisque vineam suam, et unusquisque ficum suam, et bibite unusquisque aquam cisternæ suæ,

** Isaiah 36:17

donec veniam, et tollam vos ad terram quæ est ut terra vestra, terram frumenti et vini, terram panum et vinearum.

** Isaiah 36:18

Nec conturbet vos Ezechias, dicens : Dominus liberabit nos. Numquid liberaverunt dii gentium unusquisque terram suam de manu regis Assyriorum ?

** Isaiah 36:19

Ubi est deus Emath et Arphad ? ubi est deus Sepharvaim ? numquid liberaverunt Samariam de manu mea ?

** Isaiah 36:20

Quis est ex omnibus diis terrarum istarum qui eruerit terram suam de manu mea, ut eruat Dominus Jerusalem de manu mea ?

** Isaiah 36:21

Et siluerunt, et non responderunt ei verbum. Mandaverat enim rex, dicens : Ne respondeatis ei.

** Isaiah 36:22

Et ingressus est Eliacim, filius Helciæ, qui erat super domum, et Sobna scriba, et Joahe filius Asaph, a commentariis, ad Ezechiam, scissis vestibus, et nuntiaverunt ei verba Rabsacis.  <chapter eID="Isa.36"/> <div eID="gen20415" type="x-p"/>

* Isaiah 37

** Isaiah 37:1

Et factum est, cum audisset rex Ezechias, scidit vestimenta sua, et obvolutus est sacco, et intravit in domum Domini.

** Isaiah 37:2

Et misit Eliacim, qui erat super domum, et Sobnam scribam, et seniores de sacerdotibus, opertos saccis, ad Isaiam, filium Amos, prophetam,

** Isaiah 37:3

et dixerunt ad eum : Hæc dicit Ezechias : Dies tribulationis, et correptionis, et blasphemiæ, dies hæc ; quia venerunt filii usque ad partum, et virtus non est pariendi.

** Isaiah 37:4

Si quomodo audiat Dominus Deus tuus verba Rabsacis, quem misit rex Assyriorum dominus suus ad blasphemandum Deum viventem et exprobrandum sermonibus quos audivit Dominus Deus tuus : leva ergo orationem pro reliquiis quæ repertæ sunt.

** Isaiah 37:5

Et venerunt servi regis Ezechiæ ad Isaiam.

** Isaiah 37:6

Et dixit ad eos Isaias : Hæc dicetis domino vestro : Hæc dicit Dominus : Ne timeas a facie verborum quæ audisti, quibus blasphemaverunt pueri regis Assyriorum me.

** Isaiah 37:7

Ecce ego dabo ei spiritum, et audiet nuntium, et revertetur ad terram suam, et corruere eum faciam gladio in terra sua.  <div eID="gen20416" type="x-p"/>

** Isaiah 37:8

Reversus est autem Rabsaces, et invenit regem Assyriorum præliantem adversus Lobnam : audierat enim quia profectus esset de Lachis.

** Isaiah 37:9

Et audivit de Tharaca rege Æthiopiæ, dicentes : Egressus est ut pugnet contra te. Quod cum audisset, misit nuntios ad Ezechiam, dicens :

** Isaiah 37:10

Hæc dicetis Ezechiæ regi Judæ, loquentes : Non te decipiat Deus tuus in quo tu confidis, dicens : Non dabitur Jerusalem in manu regis Assyriorum.

** Isaiah 37:11

Ecce tu audisti omnia quæ fecerunt reges Assyriorum omnibus terris, quas subverterunt : et tu poteris liberari ?

** Isaiah 37:12

Numquid eruerunt eos dii gentium quos subverterunt patres mei, Gozam, et Haram, et Reseph, et filios Eden qui erant in Thalassar ?

** Isaiah 37:13

Ubi est rex Emath, et rex Arphad, et rex urbis Sepharvaim, Ana, et Ava ?  <div eID="gen20417" type="x-p"/>

** Isaiah 37:14

Et tulit Ezechias libros de manu nuntiorum, et legit eos, et ascendit in domum Domini, et expandit eos Ezechias coram Domino :

** Isaiah 37:15

et oravit Ezechias ad Dominum, dicens :

** Isaiah 37:16

Domine exercituum, Deus Israël, qui sedes super cherubim, tu es Deus solus omnium regnorum terræ : tu fecisti cælum et terram.

** Isaiah 37:17

Inclina, Domine, aurem tuam, et audi ; aperi, Domine, oculos tuos, et vide : et audi omnia verba Sennacherib, quæ misit ad blasphemandum Deum viventem.

** Isaiah 37:18

Vere enim, Domine, desertas fecerunt reges Assyriorum terras, et regiones earum,

** Isaiah 37:19

et dederunt deos earum igni : non enim erant dii, sed opera manuum hominum, lignum et lapis, et comminuerunt eos.

** Isaiah 37:20

Et nunc, Domine Deus noster, salva nos de manu ejus, et cognoscant omnia regna terræ quia tu es Dominus solus.

** Isaiah 37:21

Et misit Isaias, filius Amos, ad Ezechiam, dicens : Hæc dicit Dominus Deus Israël : Pro quibus rogasti me de Sennacherib, rege Assyriorum,

** Isaiah 37:22

hoc est verbum quod locutus est Dominus super eum : <div eID="gen20418" type="x-p"/> <lg sID="gen20419"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20420"/>Despexit te et subsannavit te, <l eID="gen20420" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20421"/>virgo filia Sion ; <l eID="gen20421" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20422"/>post te caput movit, <l eID="gen20422" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20423"/>filia Jerusalem. <l eID="gen20423" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 37:23

Cui exprobrasti ? et quem blasphemasti ? <l eID="gen20424" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20425"/>et super quem exaltasti vocem, <l eID="gen20425" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20426"/>et levasti altitudinem oculorum tuorum ? <l eID="gen20426" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20427"/>ad Sanctum Israël. <l eID="gen20427" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 37:24

In manu servorum tuorum exprobrasti Domino, <l eID="gen20428" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20429"/>et dixisti : In multitudine quadrigarum mearum <l eID="gen20429" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20430"/>ego ascendi altitudinem montium juga Libani ; <l eID="gen20430" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20431"/>et succidam excelsa cedrorum ejus, <l eID="gen20431" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20432"/>et electas abietes illius, <l eID="gen20432" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20433"/>et introibo altitudinem summitatis ejus, <l eID="gen20433" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20434"/>saltum Carmeli ejus. <l eID="gen20434" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 37:25

Ego fodi, et bibi aquam, <l eID="gen20435" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20436"/>et exsiccavi vestigio pedis mei <l eID="gen20436" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20437"/>omnes rivos aggerum. <l eID="gen20437" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 37:26

Numquid non audisti quæ olim fecerim ei ? <l eID="gen20438" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20439"/>Ex diebus antiquis ego plasmavi illud ; <l eID="gen20439" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20440"/>et nunc adduxi, <l eID="gen20440" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20441"/>et factum est in eradicationem collium compugnantium, <l eID="gen20441" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20442"/>et civitatum munitarum. <l eID="gen20442" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 37:27

** Isaiah 37:28

Habitationem tuam, et egressum tuum, <l eID="gen20449" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20450"/>et introitum tuum cognovi, <l eID="gen20450" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20451"/>et insaniam tuam contra me. <l eID="gen20451" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 37:29

Cum fureres adversum me, <l eID="gen20452" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20453"/>superbia tua ascendit in aures meas. <l eID="gen20453" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20454"/>Ponam ergo circulum in naribus tuis, <l eID="gen20454" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20455"/>et frenum in labiis tuis, <l eID="gen20455" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20456"/>et reducam te in viam <l eID="gen20456" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20457"/>per quem venisti. <l eID="gen20457" level="1"/> <lg eID="gen20419"/>

** Isaiah 37:30

Tibi autem hoc erit signum : comede hoc anno quæ sponte nascuntur, et in anno secundo pomis vescere ; in anno autem tertio seminate et metite, et plantate vineas, et comedite fructum earum.

** Isaiah 37:31

Et mittet id quod salvatum fuerit de domo Juda, et quod reliquum est, radicem deorsum, et faciet fructum sursum :

** Isaiah 37:32

quia de Jerusalem exibunt reliquiæ, et salvatio de monte Sion : zelus Domini exercituum faciet istud.

** Isaiah 37:33

Propterea hæc dicit Dominus de rege Assyriorum : <div eID="gen20458" type="x-p"/> <lg sID="gen20459"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20460"/>Non intrabit civitatem hanc, <l eID="gen20460" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20461"/>et non jaciet ibi sagittam, <l eID="gen20461" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20462"/>et non occupabit eam clypeus, <l eID="gen20462" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20463"/>et non mittet in circuitu ejus aggerem. <l eID="gen20463" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 37:34

In via qua venit, per eam revertetur, <l eID="gen20464" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20465"/>et civitatem hanc non ingredietur, dicit Dominus. <l eID="gen20465" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 37:35

Et protegam civitatem istam, ut salvem eam <l eID="gen20466" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20467"/>propter me, et propter David, servum meum.

** Isaiah 37:36

Egressus est autem angelus Domini, et percussit in castris Assyriorum centum octoginta quinque millia. Et surrexerunt mane, et ecce omnes cadavera mortuorum.

** Isaiah 37:37

Et egressus est, et abiit, et reversus est Sennacherib, rex Assyriorum, et habitavit in Ninive.

** Isaiah 37:38

Et factum est, cum adoraret in templo Nesroch deum suum, Adramelech et Sarasar, filii ejus, percusserunt eum gladio, fugeruntque in terram Ararat ; et regnavit Asarhaddon, filius ejus, pro eo. <l eID="gen20467" level="1"/><lg eID="gen20459"/> <chapter eID="Isa.37"/>

* Isaiah 38

** Isaiah 38:1

In diebus illis ægrotavit Ezechias usque ad mortem ; et introivit ad eum Isaias, filius Amos, propheta, et dixit ei : Hæc dicit Dominus : Dispone domui tuæ, quia morieris tu, et non vives.

** Isaiah 38:2

Et convertit Ezechias faciem suam ad parietem, et oravit ad Dominum,

** Isaiah 38:3

et dixit : Obsecro, Domine, memento, quæso, quomodo ambulaverim coram te in veritate et in corde perfecto, et quod bonum est in oculis tuis fecerim. Et flevit Ezechias fletu magno.

** Isaiah 38:4

Et factum est verbum Domini ad Isaiam, dicens :

** Isaiah 38:5

Vade, et dic Ezechiæ : Hæc dicit Dominus Deus David patris tui : Audivi orationem tuam, et vidi lacrimas tuas ; ecce ego adjiciam super dies tuos quindecim annos,

** Isaiah 38:6

et de manu regis Assyriorum eruam te, et civitatem istam, et protegam eam.

** Isaiah 38:7

Hoc autem tibi erit signum a Domino, quia faciet Dominus verbum hoc quod locutus est :

** Isaiah 38:8

ecce ego reverti faciam umbram linearum per quas descenderat in horologio Achaz in sole, retrorsum decem lineis. Et reversus est sol decem lineis per gradus quos descenderat.  <div eID="gen20468" type="x-p"/>

** Isaiah 38:9

Scriptura Ezechiæ, regis Juda, cum ægrotasset et convaluisset de infirmitate sua.  <div eID="gen20469" type="x-p"/>

** Isaiah 38:10

Ego dixi in dimidio dierum meorum : <l eID="gen20471" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20472"/>Vadam ad portas inferi ; <l eID="gen20472" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20473"/>quæsivi residuum annorum meorum. <l eID="gen20473" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 38:11

Dixi : Non videbo Dominum Deum <l eID="gen20474" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20475"/>in terra viventium ; <l eID="gen20475" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20476"/>non aspiciam hominem ultra, <l eID="gen20476" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20477"/>et habitatorem quietis. <l eID="gen20477" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 38:12

Generatio mea ablata est, et convoluta est a me, <l eID="gen20478" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20479"/>quasi tabernaculum pastorum. <l eID="gen20479" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20480"/>Præcisa est velut a texente vita mea ; <l eID="gen20480" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20481"/>dum adhuc ordirer, succidit me : <l eID="gen20481" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20482"/>de mane usque ad vesperam finies me. <l eID="gen20482" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 38:13

Sperabam usque ad mane ; <l eID="gen20483" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20484"/>quasi leo, sic contrivit omnia ossa mea : <l eID="gen20484" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20485"/>de mane usque ad vesperam finies me. <l eID="gen20485" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 38:14

Sicut pullus hirundinis, sic clamabo ; <l eID="gen20486" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20487"/>meditabor ut columba. <l eID="gen20487" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20488"/>Attenuati sunt oculi mei, suspicientes in excelsum. <l eID="gen20488" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20489"/>Domine, vim patior : responde pro me. <l eID="gen20489" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 38:15

Quid dicam, aut quid respondebit mihi, <l eID="gen20490" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20491"/>cum ipse fecerit ? <l eID="gen20491" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20492"/>Recogitabo tibi omnes annos meos <l eID="gen20492" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20493"/>in amaritudine animæ meæ. <l eID="gen20493" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 38:16

Domine, si sic vivitur, <l eID="gen20494" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20495"/>et in talibus vita spiritus mei, <l eID="gen20495" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20496"/>corripies me, et vivificabis me. <l eID="gen20496" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 38:17

Ecce in pace amaritudo mea amarissima. <l eID="gen20497" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20498"/>Tu autem eruisti animam meam <l eID="gen20498" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20499"/>ut non periret ; <l eID="gen20499" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20500"/>projecisti post tergum tuum <l eID="gen20500" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20501"/>omnia peccata mea. <l eID="gen20501" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 38:18

Quia non infernus confitebitur tibi, <l eID="gen20502" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20503"/>neque mors laudabit te : <l eID="gen20503" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20504"/>non exspectabunt qui descendunt in lacum <l eID="gen20504" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen20505"/>veritatem tuam. <l eID="gen20505" level="1"/>

** Isaiah 38:21

** Isaiah 38:22

* Isaiah 39

** Isaiah 39:1

In tempore illo misit Merodach Baladan, filius Baladan, rex Babylonis, libros et munera ad Ezechiam : audierat enim quod ægrotasset et convaluisset.

** Isaiah 39:2

Lætatus est autem super eis Ezechias, et ostendit eis cellam aromatum, et argenti, et auri, et odoramentorum, et unguenti optimi, et omnes apothecas supellectilis suæ, et universa quæ inventa sunt in thesauris ejus. Non fuit verbum quod non ostenderet eis Ezechias in domo sua, et in omni potestate sua.

** Isaiah 39:3

Introivit autem Isaias propheta ad Ezechiam regem, et dixit ei : Quid dixerunt viri isti, et unde venerunt ad te ? Et dixit Ezechias : De terra longinqua venerunt ad me, de Babylone.

** Isaiah 39:4

Et dixit : Quid viderunt in domo tua ? Et dixit Ezechias : Omnia quæ in domo mea sunt viderunt ; non fuit res quam non ostenderim eis in thesauris meis.

** Isaiah 39:5

Et dixit Isaias ad Ezechiam : Audi verbum Domini exercituum.

** Isaiah 39:6

Ecce dies venient, et auferentur omnia quæ in domo tua sunt, et quæ thesaurizaverunt patres tui usque ad diem hanc, in Babylonem ; non relinquetur quidquam, dicit Dominus.

** Isaiah 39:7

Et de filiis tuis, qui exibunt de te, quos genueris, tollent, et erunt eunuchi in palatio regis Babylonis.

** Isaiah 39:8

Et dixit Ezechias ad Isaiam : Bonum verbum Domini, quod locutus est. Et dixit : Fiat tantum pax et veritas in diebus meis !  <chapter eID="Isa.39"/>
